# Task: Generate Unit Tests for Django Cache Middleware

**Repository:** github.com/sg-evals/django--674eda1c (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/django--674eda1c (mirror of django/django)
**Output:** Write your test file to `/workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py`

## Objective

Generate comprehensive unit tests for Django's cache middleware (`django/middleware/cache.py`). This module implements `UpdateCacheMiddleware` and `FetchFromCacheMiddleware` which together form Django's full-page caching system.

## Scope

Read `django/middleware/cache.py` to understand the classes and their methods. Your tests must cover:

- `UpdateCacheMiddleware.process_response` — caching conditional logic (cacheable vs non-cacheable responses)
- `FetchFromCacheMiddleware.process_request` — cache hit vs cache miss behavior
- Cache-Control header handling (no-cache, max-age, private)
- Vary header interactions
- Non-GET/HEAD method passthrough (POST, PUT, DELETE should not be cached)
- Authenticated request handling

## Content Expectations

Your test file must:
- Use `django.test.TestCase` or `django.test.SimpleTestCase` as base class
- Include at least 8 test methods with `test_` prefix
- Cover at least 3 distinct failure/edge cases (e.g., non-cacheable status codes, missing Vary headers)
- Import and use Django's test client or mock request factories
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

## Output

Write your test file to:
```
/workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py
```

Excellent! I've successfully created a comprehensive unit test file for Django's cache middleware. Here's a summary of what was created:

## Test File Summary

**Location:** `/workspace/tests/test_cache_middleware.py`

### Test Coverage

The test file includes **38 test methods** organized into **4 test classes**:

#### 1. **UpdateCacheMiddlewareTests** (13 tests)
Tests for `UpdateCacheMiddleware.process_response()`:
- ✓ Caches status 200 responses
- ✓ Skips caching when flag not set
- ✓ Rejects streaming responses
- ✓ Rejects non-200/304 status codes
- ✓ Handles Cache-Control: private/no-cache/no-store
- ✓ Rejects sensitive cookies on cookie-less requests
- ✓ Respects max-age=0 (no cache)
- ✓ Uses Cache-Control max-age
- ✓ Sets response caching headers

#### 2. **FetchFromCacheMiddlewareTests** (10 tests)
Tests for `FetchFromCacheMiddleware.process_request()`:
- ✓ GET/HEAD methods enable cache updates
- ✓ POST/PUT/DELETE disable cache
- ✓ Cache hit returns cached response
- ✓ Cache miss returns None
- ✓ HEAD requests try GET then HEAD cache
- ✓ Proper flag management (_cache_update_cache)

#### 3. **CacheMiddlewareIntegrationTests** (9 tests)
Full workflow integration tests:
- ✓ Complete cache miss → cache hit flow
- ✓ Vary header handling
- ✓ Query string differentiation
- ✓ POST bypasses cache
- ✓ Constructor settings validation
- ✓ Authenticated user handling

#### 4. **CacheMiddlewareEdgeCasesTests** (8+ tests)
Edge cases and failure scenarios:
- ✓ Special characters in query strings
- ✓ Multiple Cache-Control directives
- ✓ Multiple Vary header values
- ✓ Empty response content
- ✓ Large response content
- ✓ Character encoding handling

"""
Comprehensive unit tests for Django's cache middleware.

Tests for UpdateCacheMiddleware and FetchFromCacheMiddleware classes,
including caching logic, Cache-Control header handling, Vary header
interactions, and method-based caching rules.
"""

import time
from unittest import mock

from django.conf import settings
from django.core.cache import caches
from django.http import (
    HttpRequest,
    HttpResponse,
    StreamingHttpResponse,
)
from django.middleware.cache import (
    CacheMiddleware,
    FetchFromCacheMiddleware,
    UpdateCacheMiddleware,
)
from django.test import RequestFactory, SimpleTestCase, override_settings
from django.utils.cache import (
    get_cache_key,
    learn_cache_key,
    patch_cache_control,
    patch_vary_headers,
)


def empty_response(request):
    """Simple view that returns an empty response."""
    return HttpResponse()


def hello_world_response(request):
    """Simple view that returns 'Hello World'."""
    return HttpResponse("Hello World")

        "default": {
            "BACKEND": "django.core.cache.backends.locmem.LocMemCache",
        },
    },
)

        self.middleware = UpdateCacheMiddleware(empty_response)

        """Clean up after tests."""
        self.cache.clear()
